msg:The rooms and hotel itself are gorgeous. Very beautiful and quiet hotel. There is some construction around the hotel right now. Many things are being built but you don’t hear it. The rooms are sound proof. Some of the nicer rooms have a large round bathtub, others have a smaller oval bathtub. Best to tell the hotel which you prefer I think. The breakfast was great, be sure to add it onto your room. The staff was absolutely amazing! Maggie and Barton were incredibly helpful throughout our parties entire trip. They helped us order taxis and locate places for things we needed. I think the amenities are very nice and clean but are an extra charge to use and have some restrictive rules, such as being required to wear a swim cap in the pool. I think this hotel is more for business travelers, the rooms offer great work space and the hotel offers great meeting spaces.

Service- all staff that we interacted with were well mannered, courteous, and kind. They speak English and are very accommodating as well.

We were warmly greeted at the front desk by Maggie and Barton who went above and beyond to assist us throughout our stay. They were just a text message away at any hour. We got an upgrade to the executive suite which had a big room space and a nice view. 
The mini bar was stocked but the items were at an additional cost. The hotel boasts quite a few amenities but at an additional cost.

name:詹‍弘‍道
info:Superior Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Other
info:5 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted May 25, 2024
msg:Breakfast is rich and great!
The dining environment is very good!

I have almost never photographed restaurants^the corpse of food^, and even food is just a necessity for me to survive.
But if Chinese food elements can be added to Chinese restaurants, it will make people’s eyes brighten and come back again and again!
This is rice roll, as big as a ********* egg pancake. Add a little salt and soy sauce to enhance the flavor, it tastes good.
Disadvantages: The pastry is too thick and the fillings are too little. If the shrimps are thin-skinned, it will remind me of Hong Kong-style rice rolls.

I ate 3 bowls of raw porridge. The first bowl is preserved egg and lean meat porridge, and the second bowl is beef porridge. Eat freshly cooked porridge for breakfast, which warms my Oriental stomach. Very tasty!
The disadvantage is: this is really porridge. Whether it is preserved eggs, lean meat or beef, you have to use a magnifying glass to look for it in the porridge.
For the third bowl, I asked the freshly cooked chef to cook another bowl of beef porridge, but the amount of beef must be tripled.
This time, it’s really the beef porridge I want.

msg:Because I bought a ticket for the Youth Olympics concert at short notice, I chose Hualuxe Hotel because it was close to the Youth Olympics Pavilion. I read the reviews of several guests, and the actual experience and stay experience were even more positive.
First of all, it is very suitable for watching concerts. It is just across the Rainbow Bridge from the venue. For those with fast feet like me, it takes less than 4 minutes to get from the hotel to the stadium. (The hotel will open the Rainbow Bridge within a certain time period after receiving the notice of the performance.) There is no need to worry about the journey back to the hotel after the performance. After watching the show, I went back to the hotel to take a bath and sleep. It was very convenient and safe.
Secondly, I was very lucky that Manager Li received me during check-in. He is very considerate and provides convenience for the guests. He is considerate, clear in thinking, kind and courteous, and makes people feel very comfortable. He makes the guests feel at home on the front line. During my stay, I met him every day to say hello. After checking out, I waited for him to say goodbye and thanked him for taking care of me during this period.
Again, the two-bedroom suite is really suitable for families. The room is large, spacious, clean, and has a good view. You can see the two Youth Olympic venues and the Rainbow Bridge outside the window, and the small football field on the other side. The bathroom facilities are complete and the hardware has reached five-star standards.
Finally, let’s talk about catering. Because of the executive trea**ent, all three meals and afternoon tea are in the hotel. The breakfast was indeed as everyone reported, very rich, with a wide range of choices and Cantonese characteristics. Afternoon tea is at the lobby bar, dinner is at Eheng, until 8 pm. I go to see a show or go out for fun, and my elderly family members stay in the hotel to enjoy food and rest, which is very reassuring.
All in all, I made a wise choice this time and had a great experience. I would recommend it to everyone.

msg:Arrived at the store at 17:00 on Saturday night and had to queue for 3.40 minutes to check in. A large procession of three or four lines. The hall was noisy. Extremely slow! Considering that there is a concert, it is understandable, but it is not very efficient. There is no sense of coordination between the front desk and the housekeeping depar**ent. I don't even know how many rooms can be released when I call to ask.
Booked 2 double rooms with river view. I could only give it to one room first, and then give it to the other one around 19 o'clock. Still after urging once. There was no indication. The two rooms were said to be arranged on the same floor. Good guy, they were at opposite ends of the entire hotel. From the river view room, the first thing that caught my eye was the hotel opposite.
The parking lot 🅿️ is also unreasonable. Maybe because there are so many people, we can only park underground, and then the underground parking space is far away, which is inconvenient. You can scan the code at the front desk to park your car, it's free. There is no direct elevator to the lobby in the parking lot.
Breakfast is on the same floor as the lobby on the second floor. It's quite rich. There are a lot of people... around 9 o'clock, there are basically no seats available. You have to ask the employees for coffee, and the employees are very busy and exhausted. I use the automatic coffee machine to make latte all the time. Why not do it yourself like other hotels. You don’t need to draw flowers or anything.
All in all, there is no service to speak of. Maybe it has something to do with too many people. Not good value for money.
I didn’t go to the swimming pool. According to family members, the water was cold at about 30 degrees.
There are no rides for children (except for a little slide and rocking horse at breakfast). Not very parent-child friendly. Not recommended.
There is nothing to eat around and there are no options for takeout.
It's just purely for watching the concert, so it's okay. If there is a concert, the Rainbow Bridge at the back door of the hotel will open and connect to the Youth Olympic Sports Park. I tested it myself. Turn left when you go out and walk straight. You will reach the venue within 10 minutes. It remains open until it closes one hour after the concert (ask the security guard at the bridge).

3. When I came to the Youth Olympics to watch a concert, it was very convenient to go over the Rainbow Bridge.
The hotel's service is particularly good:
1. One week before traveling, call to inquire and confirm your room type preference, whether it is a double bed or a twin bed, and make a note
2. The day before travel, call to reconfirm the room type and confirm the estimated arrival time.
3. When you check in as scheduled, the front desk informs you that an upgrade to an executive twin room has been arranged.
4. After check-in, due to the sunshine, the room temperature was high. The room service staff immediately helped open the window for ventilation and brought ice cubes to cool down, and I quickly felt comfortable.
5. The security guard has a very good attitude. He patiently answered and gave directions several times when asked for directions.
All in all, it deserves to be owned by IHG.

早餐和南京其他同檔次的酒店相比，也有不太好的地方，比如早餐的咖啡，由於必須由工作人員幫打好，所以需要排隊領取，每次衹限一杯。造成用餐高等排隊時間過長，非常浪費時間。早餐真的需要提升下，不太好吃。😂

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior River View King Bed Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:3
posted:Posted December 4, 2023
msg:這是一次糟糕的經歷，本人確認以下的評價是客觀真實且略帶個人主觀想法但絕無杜撰和捏造，也請店方和攜程不要無故刪除評論，否則將追究你們的法律責任。

我們於12月1日晚上5:50左右抵達酒店辦理入住，可以從上傳的照片裏看到，因為晚上演唱會的緣故，酒店前台人山人海。

在經歷裏一些等待之後，我們辦理完成了入住手續，並詢問了前台在哪裡可以用餐，前台告知，三樓中餐廳已經訂滿，二樓衹剩下自助餐廳和麪家。

於是我們直接前往二樓餐廳，因為演唱會7點半就要開始，我們打算吃一個簡餐就走，可是令人沒想到的是，圖中兩位工作人員非常強硬且肯定的告知，對不起，吃麪要等一個小時，你可以吃自助餐，然後我們説因為趕着去演唱會，停下來吃個自助餐根本不現實，既然入住都辦好了，總得給我們吃口飯吧，對方説那沒辦法了，這時圖中旁邊一位工作人員告知，我們行政酒廊也是開着的，168一位自助。

之後聯繫了攜程客服投訴，攜程的反應快速且處理到位，所以這裏要説的是本投訴和攜程無關，我要成呈現的是酒店的管理和應變能力是如此的糟糕。

首先，青奧體開演唱會不是第一次了，也就是説這樣的人流高峯不是第一次，酒店竟然沒有任何準備預案，五星級酒店搞得像小菜場。非但處理入住的員工速度不行，人手不夠，電腦也很慢，且對於乘客沒有分類引導，像排在我們前面的幾位都還在討價還價和詢問房間的情況，這種情況下應該由另外的工作人員帶領其到一邊慢慢談，不然後麪排隊的人急死。

第二，這樣級別的五星級酒店竟然沒有適合客人用餐的地方，活活把人逼死。請你知悉，並不是每個客人都能接受在房間裏啃外賣的，你的行政酒廊還有大量的空間，為什麼不能在緊急情況下多安排一些位子？（之後投訴了以後，收到酒店電話説可以多加一個位子給我們，可是我們已經在房間啃外賣了）二樓三樓都還有地方可以安排，為什麼要一口拒絕客人。

最後，比起排隊辦入住（其實還能忍），最不能忍的就是上述第二點沒地方用餐，每個人客人的想法不同，我寧願不要你售後賠給我這個那個，我願意花錢來消費來提升自己的生活水準，你憑什麼叫我去房間吃外賣？這就是説，這種售中的傷害是永久性的，不是售後任何補償能彌補的。

請處理一下圖中麪家兩位員工，基於個人私隱保護，圖片打了馬賽克，時間是2023.12.1晚上6:05。

本次投訴，作為我本人，其實無意接受酒店任何的補償，而且我朋友23號也要來這裏看演唱會，我就不推薦他了。就算免單了，也挽回不了你們售中的不當處理，那種不好的感覺是永久性的。

希望你們的改進落到實處，一個優秀的售中處理會比一萬個售後處理都有用。

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior River View King Bed Room
info:Stayed in April 2023
info:Family
info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 2, 2023
msg:先説服務吧，這次訂房沒有訂含早餐的，辦入住時，酒店看到我們一家四口贈送了2大2小早餐，非常周到，很感謝。入住到退房酒店服務人員一直很熱情，希望繼續保持哦，雖然我們平時都不善於交際，但出來玩遇到熱情的笑臉還是很開心愉悦的。
設施這個我要重點誇一誇，因為新家裝修我知道一套智能家居控制系統成本是比較高的,酒店房間全屋智能語音控制，不用再手動按開關，非常方便省力，完全顛覆傳統的生活習慣。
衞生這塊就是我一直是堅持定星級酒店的原因，民宿比不了，無異味也沒有衞生死角，窗明幾凈，床品乾淨整潔，沒有任何衞生瑕疵。
環境就更不用説了，在五一擁擠的南京，酒店坐落的位置非常開闊，旁邊還是個體育館，我們房間望出去還能看到兩個大型足球場。
這次南京遊玩我感受到了很多杭州沒有的體驗，公園隨處可見的露營人，河邊的釣魚人，但不雜亂，説明城市管理還是以人為本的，非常好的人文環境。真的要多出去走走，感受不同城市的風采

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Twin Room
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Friends
info:9 Reviews
rating:3
posted:Posted August 13, 2023
msg:環境：
酒店位置在長江中間的沖積洲上，和南京鬧市區一江之隔，安靜而開闊。
樓下草場養了六七匹馬，白天訓練馬術，夜裡吃草。

設施：
地下停車場免費，大堂有咖啡吧，一樓康樂中心有泳池。
房間寬敞，設施齊全，洗浴區和卧室之間用推拉門隔斷。

衞生：
不及格，房間窗簾和傢俱很多灰塵，可以看出打掃不勤，檢查敷衍，又或者客人上座率不高，所以房間很少使用。

服務：
入住期間沒有感受到任何服務，訂單包含的歡迎水果也沒有提供。
剛退房離開，就接到電話讓給酒店寫好評。

然而，這不是一篇好評。

乾燥多塵的封閉房間，讓客人呼吸難受。衞生和服務，衹給2分。

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:1 King And 2 Twin 2 Bdrm Ste River Vw
info:Stayed in June 2023
info:Friends
info:5 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted June 19, 2023
msg:總體來説是一次還不錯的入住體驗，尤其要表揚前廳部的各位，以及客房的阿姨。前期的溝通和入住的過程都很愉快，入住過程中的響應也很迅速。
但是，在離開酒店時發現了一件事，直接拉低了整式的入住評分！
我們是打車離開酒店的，接我們的出租車從酒店入口進入，在上車點等了我們半分鐘，然後我們上車，在酒店出口卻被攔下，自動收費裝置顯示要付停車費300多元，但實際上出租車是剛才進來，在酒店待的時間最多不超過三分鐘。
在這種情況下，酒店安保部毫無作為，在我出示打車軟件訂單訊息（對應車牌號）的情況下，堅持不放行，一定要請示領導。在請示領導之後，他們的領導也毫無作為，導致酒店出口車輛全部擁堵，也不説確認的情況。
最後是我打電話給前廳部，由前廳部經理過來溝通才將我們放行，最後給出的解釋僅僅是系統問題。
前後浪費了我們將近20分鐘，且不説系統問題造成的責任不應該由客人來承擔，在出現如此離譜的錯誤情況下，安保部第一時間來解決，也不為客人着想，而僅僅是堅持不放行，不應該是這樣的酒店應該有的情況！

info:Family
info:3 Reviews

posted:Posted October 3, 2022
msg:國慶不能離寧，孩子説要泡酒店，安排～
酒店在長江隧道旁邊，看似偏僻，其實交通很便捷，停車也方便，適合自駕出行。
感謝前台羅亞玲小姐姐，看見我們帶着小baby，幫我們升級了帶大浴缸的行政房，小bb泡澡很嗨。還貼心的為我們準備了嬰兒床，嬰兒床一邊可以放下圍欄緊貼大床，方便照顧，寶寶睡着很舒服，對帶小嬰兒出行的家庭特別友好。
酒店餐飲做的很不錯，不管是早餐、彩豐樓的任點任食或是行政酒廊的happy hour味道都不錯，長者和孩子吃的很滿意。
酒店位於青奧體育公園，也因此酒店的康體中心運動項目是我見過最豐富的了，有保齡球、網球、桌球、乒乓球甚至還有馬球，泳池也是可圈可點，水質很好環境清爽，還帶有一個專門的小童泳池，水温很適合小童。
酒店對面是綠水灣濕地公園，雖然沒什麼特別的，但早晚溜溜娃足夠了。
真真是一個適合全家老小泡上幾天的酒店，五星推薦！！

半夜房間燈，出現了無法控制的問題，兩點多換房。基本一個晚上沒睡起來。第二天前台的處理，就開始套路起來了。屬於欺負老實人的那種。雖然最後的處理，勉強達到了我的心理預期，但，是我開始惱火之後，一點點擠牙膏似的爭取到的。其過程很不愉快。我希望貴酒店能“好好説話就有用”，不要讓顧客“發了火”才處理。

posted:Posted February 2, 2022
msg:去年過年的時候在此入住，今年過年一家五口兩間房連住兩晚。前台服務依舊保持洲際一貫水準。這次兩間房的浴缸熱水全都不熱，導致夜裡一直肚子疼。第二天反映後浴缸熱水有改善，工作人員積極改進並電話詢問入住感受，很贊！
但第二天也就是大年夜的自助晚餐忍不住想吐槽：1、作為酒店大年夜的晚餐，無論在品種上還是在品質上明顯過於敷衍。雖然有蝦 魷魚 海螺等海鮮 但全部為冷凍的 這也無可厚非 但都沒有怎麼解凍就放在自取區我還是第一次遇見 2、海鮮區加工燒烤或爆炒基本都沒有怎麼入味或煮熟，這是因為本身食物沒有怎麼解凍導致，晚餐後家裡兩位成員拉肚子，一位胃疼3、作為當晚308一位的自助餐價格明顯名不副實，當晚迎賓一位長呢子大衣女看到小孩追着要確認154元小孩費用，態度生硬且傲慢。總之當晚是一次非常不愉快的體驗。有點諷刺的是，大年初一的早餐，這位女管理員下班之際，自己在自助區竟拿了兩大包食物帶回家。不知道是不是可以直接在後廚區進行，畢竟客人都在吃早餐，這波操作實屬不妥，個人意見。酒店管理仍需完善。
除了餐飲方面，禮賓部各位都非常棒，新年期間堅守崗位，非常盡心，祝新年快樂
